dark:text-gray-400\">Installation</p><h1 class=\"mt-2 text-3xl font-medium tracking-tight text-gray-950 dark:text-white\">Get started with Tailwind CSS</h1><p data-description=\"true\" class=\"mt-6 text-base/7 text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300\">Tailwind CSS works by scanning all of your HTML files, JavaScript components, and any other templates for class names, generating the corresponding styles and then writing them to a static CSS file.</p><p class=\"mt-4 text-base/7 text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300\">It's fast, flexible, and reliable \u2014 with zero-runtime.</p><div class=\"mt-10\" data-content=\"true\"><section class=\"relative mb-16\"><div class=\"relative z-10\"><h2 data-docsearch-ignore=\"true\" class=\"mb-6 text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-gray-950 CDN</a></h2></li></ul></div></div></div><div id=\"content-wrapper\" class=\"prose relative z-10 mb-10 max-w-3xl\" data-content=\"true\"><h3 data-title=\"true\" class=\"sr-only\">Installing Tailwind CSS as a Vite plugin</h3><p>Installing Tailwind CSS as a Vite plugin is the most seamless way to integrate it with frameworks like Laravel, SvelteKit, React Router, Nuxt, and SolidJS.</p></div><div class=\"grid grid-cols-[auto_repeat(5,minmax(0,1fr))] gap-x-6 xl:gap-y-10\"><div><div class=\"grid size-7 grid-cols-1 grid-rows-1 place-content-center border-1 border-gray-700/50 font-mono SvelteKit, React Router, Nuxt, and SolidJS.</p></div><div class=\"grid grid-cols-[auto_repeat(5,minmax(0,1fr))] gap-x-6 xl:gap-y-10\"><div><div class=\"grid size-7 grid-cols-1 grid-rows-1 href=\"/docs/transform-origin\">transform-origin</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/transform-style\">transform-style</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/translate\">translate</a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n<div>\n<h3>Interactivity</h3>\n<ul>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/accent-color\">accent-color</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/appearance\">appearance</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/caret-color\">caret-color</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/color-scheme\">color-scheme</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/cursor\">cursor</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/field-sizing\">field-sizing</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/pointer-events\">pointer-events</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/resize\">resize</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/scroll-behavior\">scroll-behavior</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/scroll-margin\">scroll-margin</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/scroll-padding\">scroll-padding</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/scroll-snap-align\">scroll-snap-align</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/scroll-snap-stop\">scroll-snap-stop</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/scroll-snap-type\">scroll-snap-type</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/touch-action\">touch-action</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/user-select\">user-select</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/will-change\">will-change</a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n<div>\n<h3>SVG</h3>\n<ul>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/fill\">fill</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/stroke\">stroke</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"/docs/stroke-width\">stroke-width</a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n<div>\n<h3>Accessibility</h3>\n<ul><li><a href=\"/docs/forced-color-adjust\">forced-color-adjust</a></li></ul>\n</div></nav></div></div></div></div>\n<div><div><div>\n<p>Installation</p>\n<h1>Get started with Tailwind CSS</h1>\n<p>Tailwind CSS works by scanning all of your HTML files, JavaScript components, and any other templates for class names, generating the corresponding styles and then writing them to a static CSS file.</p>\n<p>It's fast, flexible, and reliable \u2014 with zero-runtime.</p>\n<div><section><div>\n<h2>Installation</h2>\n<div><div><ul>\n<li><h2><a href=\"/docs/installation/using-vite\">Using Vite</a></h2></li>\n<li><h2><a href=\"/docs/installation/using-postcss\">Using PostCSS</a></h2></li>\n<li><h2><a href=\"/docs/installation/tailwind-cli\">Tailwind CLI</a></h2></li>\n<li><h2><a href=\"/docs/installation/framework-guides\">Framework Guides</a></h2></li>\n<li><h2><a href=\"/docs/installation/play-cdn\">Play CDN</a></h2></li>\n</ul></div></div>\n</div>\n<div>\n<h3>Installing Tailwind CSS as a Vite plugin</h3>\n<p>Installing Tailwind CSS as a Vite plugin is the most seamless way to integrate it with frameworks like Laravel, SvelteKit, React Router, Nuxt, and SolidJS.</p>\n</div>\n<div>\n<div><div><div>01</div></div></div>\n<div>\n<h4>Create your project</h4>\n<div><p>Start by creating a new Vite project if you don\u2019t have one set up already. The most common approach is to use<!-- --> <a href=\"https://vite.dev/guide/#scaffolding-your-first-vite-project\">Create Vite</a>.</p></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>Terminal</div>\n<div><pre><code><span><span>npm</span><span> create</span><span> vite@latest</span><span> my-project</span></span><span><span>cd</span><span> my-project</span></span></code></pre></div>\n</div></div></div>\n<div><div><div>02</div></div></div>\n<div>\n<h4>Install Tailwind CSS</h4>\n<div><p>Install <code>tailwindcss</code> and <code>@tailwindcss/vite</code> via npm.</p></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>Terminal</div>\n<div><pre><code><span><span>npm</span><span> install</span><span> tailwindcss</span><span> @tailwindcss/vite</span></span></code></pre></div>\n</div></div></div>\n<div><div><div>03</div></div></div>\n<div>\n<h4>Configure the Vite plugin</h4>\n<div><p>Add the <code>@tailwindcss/vite</code> plugin to your Vite configuration.</p></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>vite.config.ts</div>\n<div><pre><code><span><span>import</span><span> {</span><span> defineConfig</span><span> }</span><span> from</span><span> 'vite'</span></span><span><span>import</span><span> tailwindcss</span><span> from</span><span> '@tailwindcss/vite'</span></span><span><span>export</span><span> default</span><span> defineConfig</span><span>(</span><span>{</span></span><span><span> plugins</span><span>:</span><span> [</span></span><span><span> tailwindcss</span><span>()</span><span>,</span></span><span><span> ]</span><span>,</span></span><span><span>}</span><span>)</span></span></code></pre></div>\n</div></div></div>\n<div><div><div>04</div></div></div>\n<div>\n<h4>Import Tailwind CSS</h4>\n<div><p>Add an <code>@import</code> to your CSS file that imports Tailwind CSS.</p></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>CSS</div>\n<div><pre><code><span><span>@import</span><span> \"tailwindcss\"</span><span>;</span></span></code></pre></div>\n</div></div></div>\n<div><div><div>05</div></div></div>\n<div>\n<h4>Start your build process</h4>\n<div><p>Run your build process with <code>npm run dev</code> or whatever command is configured in your<!-- --> <code>package.json</code> file.</p></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>Terminal</div>\n<div><pre><code><span><span>npm</span><span> run</span><span> dev</span></span></code></pre></div>\n</div></div></div>\n<div><div><div>06</div></div></div>\n<div>\n<h4>Start using Tailwind in your HTML</h4>\n<div><p>Make sure your compiled CSS is included in the <code>&lt;head&gt;</code> <em>(your framework might handle this for you)</em>, then start using Tailwind\u2019s utility classes to style your content.</p></div>\n</div>\n<div><div><div>\n<div>HTML</div>\n<div><pre><code><span><span>&lt;!</span><span>doctype</span><span> html</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span>&lt;</span><span>html</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span>&lt;</span><span>head</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span> &lt;</span><span>meta</span><span> charset</span><span>=</span><span>\"UTF-8\"</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span> &lt;</span><span>meta</span><span> name</span><span>=</span><span>\"viewport\"</span><span> content</span><span>=</span><span>\"width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0\"</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span> &lt;</span><span>link</span><span> href</span><span>=</span><span>\"/src/style.css\"</span><span> rel</span><span>=</span><span>\"stylesheet\"</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span>&lt;/</span><span>head</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span>&lt;</span><span>body</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span> &lt;</span><span>h1</span><span> class</span><span>=</span><span>\"text-3xl font-bold underline\"</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span> Hello world!</span></span><span><span> &lt;/</span><span>h1</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span>&lt;/</span><span>body</span><span>&gt;</span></span><span><span>&lt;/</span><span>html</span><span>&gt;</span></span></code></pre></div>\n</div></div></div>\n</div>\n<div><div>\n<div><span><strong>Are you stuck?</strong> Setting up Tailwind with Vite can be a bit different across different build tools. Check our framework guides to see if we have more specific instructions for your particular setup.</span></div>\n<div><a href=\"/docs/installation/framework-guides\">Explore our framework guides</a></div>\n</div></div>\n<!--$--><!--/$--></section></div>\n</div></div></div>\n<div><footer><div>\n<div>\n<div>\n<h3>Tailwind CSS</h3>\n<ul>\n<li><a [forced-color-adjust](https://tailwindcss.com/docs/forced-color-adjust)\n\n\nInstallation\n# Get started with Tailwind CSS\nTailwind CSS works by scanning all of your HTML files, JavaScript components, and any other templates for class names, generating the corresponding styles and then writing them to a static CSS file.\nIt's fast, flexible, and reliable \u2014 with zero-runtime.\n## Installation\n * ## [Using Vite](https://tailwindcss.com/docs/installation/using-vite)\n * ## [Using PostCSS](https://tailwindcss.com/docs/installation/using-postcss)\n * ## [Tailwind CLI](https://tailwindcss.com/docs/installation/tailwind-cli)\n * ## [Framework Guides](https://tailwindcss.com/docs/installation/framework-guides)\n \* ## [Play CDN](https://tailwindcss.com/docs/installation/play-cdn)\n\n\n### Installing Tailwind CSS as a Vite plugin\nInstalling Tailwind CSS as a Vite plugin is the most seamless way to integrate it with frameworks like Laravel, SvelteKit, React Router, Nuxt, and SolidJS.\n01\n#### Create your project\nStart by creating a new Vite project if you don\u2019t have one set up already. The most common approach is to use [Create Vite](https://vite.dev/guide/#scaffolding-your-first-vite-project).\nTerminal\n`\nnpm create vite@latest my-projectcd my-project\n`\n\n02\n#### Install Tailwind CSS\nInstall `tailwindcss` and `@tailwindcss/vite` via npm.\nTerminal\n`\nnpm install tailwindcss @tailwindcss/vite\n`\n\n03\n#### Configure the Vite plugin\nAdd the `@tailwindcss/vite` plugin to your Vite configuration.\nvite.config.ts\n`\nimport { defineConfig } from 'vite'import tailwindcss from '@tailwindcss/vite'export default defineConfig({  plugins: [    tailwindcss(),  ],})\n`\n\n04\n#### Import Tailwind CSS\nAdd an `@import` to your CSS file that imports Tailwind CSS.\nCSS\n`\n@import \"tailwindcss\";\n`\n\n05\n#### Start your build process\nRun your build process with `npm run dev` or whatever command is configured in your `package.json` file.\nTerminal\n`\nnpm run dev\n`\n\n06\n#### Start using Tailwind in your HTML\nMake sure your compiled CSS is included in the `<head>` _(your framework might handle this for you)_ , then start using Tailwind\u2019s utility classes to style your content.\nHTML\n`\n<!doctype html><html><head>  <meta charset=\"UTF-8\">  <meta name=\"viewport\" content=\"width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0\">  <link href=\"/src/style.css\" rel=\"stylesheet\"></head><body>  <h1 class=\"text-3xl font-bold underline\">    Hello world!  </h1></body></html>\n`\n\n**Are you stuck?** Setting up Tailwind with Vite can be a bit different across different build tools. Check our framework guides to see if we have more specific instructions for your particular setup.\n[Explore our framework guides](https://tailwindcss.com/docs/installation/framework-guides)\n### forced-color-adjust\u27e8191\u27e9\n\n\nInstallation\n# Get started with Tailwind CSS\nTailwind CSS works by scanning all of your HTML files, JavaScript components, and any other templates for class names, generating the corresponding styles and then writing them to a static CSS file.\nIt's fast, flexible, and reliable \u2014 with zero-runtime.\n## Installation\n * ## Using Vite\u27e8192\u27e9\n * ## Using PostCSS\u27e8193\u27e9\n * ## Tailwind CLI\u27e8194\u27e9\n * ## Framework Guides\u27e8195\u27e9\n \* ## Play CDN\u27e8196\u27e9\n\n\n### Installing Tailwind CSS as a Vite plugin\nInstalling Tailwind CSS as a Vite plugin is the most seamless way to integrate it with frameworks like Laravel, SvelteKit, React Router, Nuxt, and SolidJS.\n01\n#### Create your project\nStart by creating a new Vite project if you don\u2019t have one set up already. The most common approach is to use Create Vite\u27e8197\u27e9.\nTerminal\n`\nnpm create vite@latest my-projectcd my-project\n`\n\n02\n#### Install Tailwind CSS\nInstall `tailwindcss` and `@tailwindcss/vite` via npm.\nTerminal\n`\nnpm install tailwindcss @tailwindcss/vite\n`\n\n03\n#### Configure the Vite plugin\nAdd the `@tailwindcss/vite` plugin to your Vite configuration.\nvite.config.ts\n`\nimport { defineConfig } from 'vite'import tailwindcss from '@tailwindcss/vite'export default defineConfig({  plugins: [    tailwindcss(),  ],})\n`\n\n04\n#### Import Tailwind CSS\nAdd an `@import` to your CSS file that imports Tailwind CSS.\nCSS\n`\n@import \"tailwindcss\";\n`\n\n05\n#### Start your build process\nRun your build process with `npm run dev` or whatever command is configured in your `package.json` file.\nTerminal\n`\nnpm run dev\n`\n\n06\n#### Start using Tailwind in your HTML\nMake sure your compiled CSS is included in the `<head>` _(your framework might handle this for you)\_ , then start using Tailwind\u2019s utility classes to style your content.\nHTML\n`\n<!doctype html><html><head>  <meta charset=\"UTF-8\">  <meta name=\"viewport\" content=\"width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0\">  <link href=\"/src/style.css\" rel=\"stylesheet\"></head><body>  <h1 class=\"text-3xl font-bold underline\">    Hello world!  </h1></body></html>\n`\n\n**Are you stuck?** Setting up Tailwind with Vite can be a bit different across different build tools. Check our framework guides to see if we have more specific instructions for your particular setup.\nExplore our framework guides\u27e8195\u27e9\n### Tailwind CSS\n _ Documentation\u27e81\u27e9\n _ Playground\u27e8198\u27e9\n _ Blog\u27e82\u27e9\n _ Showcase\u27e83\u27e9\n _ Sponsor\u27e84\u27e9\n\n\n### Resources\n _ Refactoring UI\u27e8199\u27e9\n _ Headless UI\u27e8200\u27e9\n _ Heroicons\u27e8201\u27e9\n _ Hero Patterns\u27e8202\u27e9\n\n\n### Tailwind Plus\u27e8203\u27e9\n _ UI Blocks\u27e8204\u27e9\n _ Templates\u27e8205\u27e9\n _ UI Kit\u27e8206\u27e9\n\n\n### Community\n _ GitHub\u27e8207\u27e9\n _ Discord\u27e85\u27e9\n _ X\u27e8208\u27e9\n\n\n### Tailwind CSS\n _ Documentation\u27e81\u27e9\n _ Playground\u27e8198\u27e9\n _ Blog\u27e82\u27e9\n _ Showcase\u27e83\u27e9\n _ Sponsor\u27e84\u27e9\n\n\n### Tailwind Plus\u27e8203\u27e9\n _ UI Blocks\u27e8204\u27e9\n _ Templates\u27e8205\u27e9\n _ UI Kit\u27e8206\u27e9\n\n\n### Resources\n _ Refactoring UI\u27e8199\u27e9\n _ Headless UI\u27e8200\u27e9\n _ Heroicons\u27e8201\u27e9\n _ Hero Patterns\u27e8202\u27e9\n\n\n### Community\n _ GitHub\u27e8207\u27e9\n _ Discord\u27e85\u27e9\n _ X\u27e8208\u27e9\n\n\nCopyright \u00a9 2025 Tailwind Labs Inc.\u00b7Trademark Policy\u27e8209\u27e9\n",
